10a1(dkon brtsegs): ste thab 'i spang sras nas pa mthar sprul/ ji ltar sangs rgyas mchog gi gzhi mtha' yas/ mi dbang gA'i rdzi phyogs bcur lam ser gdal/ da ltar bdag kyangs na
10a2(dkon brtsegs): rgyas rgyas rgyal gyur/ the su dag dang mchilas rab thar bgyi/ sbyi dang dus da rgyal khrims bzod/ bcon 'grus bsas sogs 'jim sa mtshab 'dul chubs 'a'angag bdun na
10a3(dkon brtsegs): yang dag blang / sems can rtsub pa sangs rgyas gyur par bgyi/ byang chub zhi mchog mtshungs med tshal bgyid cing / sangs rgyas bye brgya stong du ma'i zan/ gro gi khyi ma lta bur mtha' yas pa/ 
10a4(dkon brtsegs): mdun pa dgran radas gis mnang bar bgyi/ gang ga'i rdus dang mnyam pa'i 'jig nan khamasadabs gong du mtha' yas zhing gi nams/ de ngas kun tu'ang na za 'byin pa/ 
10a5(dkon brtsegs): 'dra'i brdzun 'grus spobs mi rnam par bgyi/ yangag gis zhing yangs mtsha thongs pa mtshas 'dus byas 'dir ni rgyan pa bgyis nasu/ mtshungs pa ma semam ma ngan sa ma
10a6(dkon brtsegs): yang ma mchis pas nirnam par sbyang / byams bcu dag nas lhags pa'i sems can rnams/ de zhugs sbyar du bde ba dga' bar 'gyuro/ sadas rgyas rang ma 'dzin bdag gi dang / 
10a7(dkon brtsegs): log brtson 'grus skabs me bstod par mtshal/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten mi chags mkhyen pa tsan/ mkhas pa de dag tu ni bdag sems mkhyen/ bdag ni mtshams med mchis ten na/ 
10a8(dkon brtsegs): gnas brtse/ sman lam tha'as las ldas ma kyang mi 'gyur/ kun dag di nas dge slong nas kyi 'byung gnas des/ com ldan 'das pa pani na gshegs pa 'jig rten dang phyug rgyas
10b1(dkon brtsegs): la/ tshigs chad pa 'di dag gis mngon su du mngon par skad nas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs/ 
10b2(dkon brtsegs): bar 'chang rgya bar 'tshal te// yang dang yang bla ni med pa yong dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed cing / yongs snga bar bgyed mchi nas kyang bdag myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs
10b3(dkon brtsegs): pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tsheng brgya thA dang / 'jig rten du de bzhin gshegs pa mi mnyam byeng mnyam par 'gyur ba de wA bu'i chos/ com ldan 'das kyis bdag la la
10b4(dkon brtsegs): par stan du gsol/ rnam pa gang dag gis bdag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yon tan gyi rgyan bkod pa yum su tshogs pa yongasu 'dzin par 'gyem bu'i rnam pa te yang ni/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
10b5(dkon brtsegs): bdag la yangasu rjod du gsol/ kun draga' de skad ces gsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'das de/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten dbang phyug rgyal po rjes/ dge slong chos kyi 'byung gnas
10b6(dkon brtsegs): de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// de'i phyi ngas slong khyod bdag nyid kyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing yon tan gyi rgyan bkod pa phun su tshogs pa yongasu bzung shig/ des gsol pa/ 
10b7(dkon brtsegs): bcom ldan 'dag smra ba ma mchis// de bzhin gshegs pa gzhan dag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yon tan bkang ba'i rgyan phun sum tshogs pa gang thos nas bdag gi rgyad thams cad yongs rgya
10b8(dkon brtsegs): par 'gyur ba/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad du gsol/ kun dga' nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs 'jig rten dbang phyug rgyal po des/ dge slo
11a1(dkon brtsegs): de'i bsem pa me khyen nas drim panang pa/ len par brags brtse ba can gis thugs byartse ba nye brgya mdzung ste/ rgyasangs rgyas kyi tshul mi gcad pa'i phyir sems can rnams la thugs rje chen po skyed/ 
11a2(dkon brtsegs): sa la bye ba tham par sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig rgya stong phrag brgya bcu rtsa na cig gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yom tan gi rgyu ma bkod pa phun su tshogs pa rnam pa dang bcas/ yul phyogs dang bcos/ gzhi ci las gyur
11a3(dkon brtsegs): pa dang bcas par yang dag par rab tu bshad // de nas bcom ldan 'das la/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' thos 'di skad ces+ya gsol te/ bcom ldan 'das 'jig rten dbang phyug rgyal po de'i sku tshe'i tshad ni ji
11a4(dkon brtsegs): zhes thun par gyur/ sems tsan gde dag skyes pa de dag thams cad 'di lta / gser / byon bcin mar gyur pa'i sring du bla na meng pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
11a5(dkon brtsegs): par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya bar mi brgya'o/ bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag gi sangs rgyas kyi'o zhing de na lha dang mi tha dad pa dag ganga' bar gyur pa gzhan du mgun rdzob kyi tha snyad tsam du ming
11a6(dkon brtsegs): du bdas lha dang mi zhes bgyi ba'i grangasu mchi bar ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla ma med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'i chang brgya bar mi bgyi ma/ bcom ldan
11a7(dkon brtsegs): 'das gal te bdag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can gang dag skyes par gyur pa de dag thams cad gal te tha na sems kyi skad cig thad cig la/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khro ga khrig brgya stong 'od ba
11a8(dkon brtsegs): rdzu 'phrul la/ dbang po'i dam pa lce la rol tu phyin par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs par 'i chung brgya bra mi brgya'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag gis sangs rgyas
11b1(dkon brtsegs): kyonang deng sems cam gang dag skyes par gyur ba de drug thams can bzlas pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya dang rje su dran pa'i rtsa bar ma rgyam bya de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byung
11b2(dkon brtsegs): chub myongan par rdzogs par 'chang brgya bar mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag gi sangs rgyas kyi zheng der sems can gang dag skyes par gyur pa dag thams cad bla na 'jig rten gyi
11b3(dkon brtsegs): bye ba khrag khrim pa rgya stong mthong ba'i lha'i mig mthong ba'i lha'i mig thob par gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par mtshung brgya bar mi gyi
11b4(dkon brtsegs): bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can gang dag skyes par rgyur pa de dag thams cad the na sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du cir che rje chos nyan pas
11b5(dkon brtsegs): lha'i rna 'thob par mu gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon pa re rdzogs pa ro 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal to// 
11b6(dkon brtsegs): bdag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can yang dag skyes pa de dag thams cad tha na/ sangs rgyas skyezhing bye ba khyim rje khros brgya stong du rtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi sems kyi spyod pa
11b7(dkon brtsegs): 'tshal bar/ pha rol gyi sems 'tshal ba la mkhas par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang drug phyi rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tsheng brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom/ 
11b8(dkon brtsegs): ldan 'das gal te bdag gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can gang dag skyes par gyur pa de dag thams cad nan+da/ rang gi lus la yong su 'dzin par 'du shes 'ga' zhig skyed na yang de srid du// 
13a1(dkon brtsegs): n+ya/ srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon na par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi
13a2(dkon brtsegs): zhing grangs ma mchis dpag tu ma mchis pa dag na/ sems can gang dag gis bdag gi ming thos nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing der skye bar bgyi ba'i slad du/ sems gtong zhing dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams kyang yongasu sngo bar
13a3(dkon brtsegs): bgyid na/ mtshams ma mchis pa bgyid pa dang / dam pa'i chos spong ba'i sgrib pas bsgribs pa'i sems can rnams ma rtogs par/ de dag tha na sems bskyed par 'gyur ba bcus sangs rgyas kyi zhing de
13a4(dkon brtsegs): skye bar ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ 
13a5(dkon brtsegs): sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can gang dag skyes par gyur pa de dag thams cad skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis dang ldan par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag
13a6(dkon brtsegs): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gas te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can gang dag skyes par gyur pa/ 
13a7(dkon brtsegs): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po go ma chen po bgos pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi don du go cha 'gos pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi don la brtson pa/ 'jig rten thams cad yongasu su
13a8(dkon brtsegs): ngan la zla ba la mngon par brtson pa/ 'jig rten gi khams thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spad pa spyod par 'tshal ba/ sangs rgyas thams cad la phud dud bgyi bar 'tshal ba/ sems can gang
13b1(dkon brtsegs): klung gi bye mo snyeng bla ma med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la dgod par 'chal ba yang gong ma'i spyod pa la mngon du phyogs pa/ kun tu bzang po'i spyod pas nges par 'byung ba rnams kyi smon lam kyi khyang
13b2(dkon brtsegs): par ma rtogs par de dag thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu skye ba gcig gis thogs par ma gyur pa da srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon
13b3(dkon brtsegs): par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can gang dag skyes par gyur pa de dag thams cad snga dro gcig bzhin sas
13b4(dkon brtsegs): rgyas kyi zhing gzhan dag tu mchis la/ sangs rgyas stong phrab mang po dang / sangs rgyas rgya stong phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas bye ba phrag ma po nas/ sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag mang po dag
13b5(dkon brtsegs): la 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus bde bar sbyar ba thams cad kyis bsnyen bkur bgyid par ma gyur pa de/ srid du/ bdog bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya/ 
13b6(dkon brtsegs): bar mi bgyi'o/ bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na byang chub seMsadapa' de dag 'di lta ste/ gser ram/ dngul lam/ nor bu 'am/ mu tig gam/ byeru
13b7(dkon brtsegs): 'am/ dung ngam/ man shel lam/ bye ru 'am/ shel lam/ spug gam/ rdo'i snying po 'am/ mu tig dmar po la stsogs pa gang yang rung ba 'am/ rin po che thams cad dam/ me tog dang / spos dang / 
13b8(dkon brtsegs): phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / bdug pa dang / phye ma dang / gos dang / bdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / mar me thams cad dang / klu dang kar dang / rol mo'i dbyangs sgra 'am/ rnam pa ji lta bu dag/ 
14a1(dkon brtsegs): n+ya// 'tshal bar gyur nas gyur nas/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams bskrun pa rnam pa de lta bu de dag/ sems bskyed ma thag tu gal te de dag la 'byung bar ma gyur pa de srid du/ bla na med pa yang dag
14a2(dkon brtsegs): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngos par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can gang skyes par gyur pa'o
14a3(dkon brtsegs): ngag thams cad/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i chos kyi bka' mchid mchi bar ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang
14a4(dkon brtsegs): brgya bar mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na byang chub sems dpa' dag 'di snyan du bdag cag 'jig rten gyi khams 'di na gnas
14a5(dkon brtsegs): bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med/ dpag tu med pa dag tu/ sangs rgyas btsam/ ldan 'das rnams la 'di lta ste/ na bza' dang / zhal zas dang / gzims cha dang
14a6(dkon brtsegs): spun gi gsos sman dang / yo byad rnams dang / me tog dang 'dug pa dang / spos dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / phye ma dang / na bza' dang / bdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / 
14a7(dkon brtsegs): da rnams dang / klu dang / gA ra dang / sil snyan dang / rin po che rnam pa tha dad pa'i chang rnams kyis/ bsti stong du bgyi ba dang / bla mar bgyi ba dang / ri mor bgyi ba dang / rim 'gror
14a8(dkon brtsegs): gyi dang / mchod par bgyi bar sems bskyed pa/ de dag gis sems bskyed ma thag tu/ gal te 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dgis thugs rtse ba nye bar bzung ste/ mchod pa/ 
14b1(dkon brtsegs): dag pa zhes par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla ma med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par ma tshang brgya bar mi bgyir// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub
14b2(dkon brtsegs): tho pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can gang dag skyes par gyur pa de dag thams cad sreng med kyi bu dang / rdo rje ltar 'khregs pa'i lus dang / mthu thob par ma gyur pa de srid du/ 
14b3(dkon brtsegs): bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par ma tshang mi rgyabargya par mi dgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi
14b4(dkon brtsegs): zhing de na rgyan gyi kha dog sems can 'ga' zhig gis lha'i mig gis mtha' lta na yang // / sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di'i gzi rnying ni 'di lta bu'o// kha dog ni 'di lta bu/ 'byor pa ni lta bu'o// 
14b5(dkon brtsegs): zhes kha dog tha dad pa dag 'tshal bar ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag pa rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'chang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gas/ 
14b6(dkon brtsegs): te bdag byang chub thab pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na thams cad kyi nang nas byang chub sems dpa' gang dge ba'i rtsa ba chung ba des kyang / byang chub kyi shing dpag tshad stong drug brgya tsam du
14b7(dkon brtsegs): mtho bar mtshal bar ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang
14b8(dkon brtsegs): chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na byang chub sems dpa' gang nod pa dang / kha don bgyid par gyur pa de dag thams cad so so yang dag par rig pa thob par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla/ 
16a1(dkon brtsegs): na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'chang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sos
16a2(dkon brtsegs): can gang dag skyes par gyur pa de dag thams cad/ shes rab dang spobs pa mtha' yas pa thob par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par
16a3(dkon brtsegs): 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing der gang na kun tu sangs rgyas kyi zhing dpag tu ma mchis/ grangs ma mchis/ bsam gyi
16a4(dkon brtsegs): mi khyag mtshungs pa ma mchis/ tshad ma mchis ngag kun tu gangar ba 'di lta ste/ dper na/ shin tu phyis pa'i me long gi dkyil 'khor la/ bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor gda' ba de
16a5(dkon brtsegs): bu'i 'od bsal 'ang ma gyur pa de snyed du/ rangag bla ma med pa yang dag par dzubs pa'i byu/ mngon par rdzogs par 'chang brgya bar mi bgyir/ bcom ldan 'das gas ta bdag
16a6(dkon brtsegs): chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na sa'i steng nas gzung ste/ bar snang gi bar las lha dang mi'i yul las shin du 'das pa'i bdug pa rigs bzang po de bzhin gshegs pa nga/ 
16a7(dkon brtsegs): byang chub sems dpa' lo 'os pa dag dri rab tu gda' ba'i pog snod rin po che sna tshogs las bgyis pa brgya stong dag nas rtag tu 'dugs par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag
16a8(dkon brtsegs): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing der de na mi rtog dri rab tu gda' ba tha dad pa'i cha
16b1(dkon brtsegs): rtag tu 'bas par ma gyur pa dang / rol ma'i dbyangs sA'i bar yid du mchi la'i sI mjug tu sgra 'thung bar ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang nges par rdzogs pa'i rlung chub mngon par
16b2(dkon brtsegs): rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te 'angs byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ bdag gi 'od kyis 'jig rten gyi khams grangs ma mchis/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ 
16b3(dkon brtsegs): mtshungs pa ma mchis pa dag tu sems can gang dag la bsal bar gyur pa de dag thams cad/ lha dang mi las shim tu 'das pa'i bde ba dang / ldan par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa
16b4(dkon brtsegs): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ kun tu sangs rgyas kyi zhing dpag tu ma
16b5(dkon brtsegs): mchis/ grangs ma mchis/ bsam gyis mi khyab/ mtshungs pa ma mchis/ tshad ma mchis pa dag tu byang chub sems dpal dag gis bdag gi ming thos te/ thos ma thag pa
16b6(dkon brtsegs): las byung ba'i dge ba'i rtsa bas che rje su nus/ byang chub kyi snying po'i mtha'i bar du gzungs thob par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par
16b7(dkon brtsegs): par 'tshang 'artsubar mi 'gyi'o// bcoM ldan 'das gal ta bangs byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ kun tu sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs ma mchis bsam gyis mi khyab mtshungs pa ma mchis/ nang ma mchis dpag tu ma mchis pa
16b8(dkon brtsegs): dag bre dra ga nga thas nas rang tung nga bsgres te/ kye chub tums bskyed 'ar gyur pa/ chung med kyi lus spang bar byar te/ de ngang marjes te cang med kyi lus lan ci nyes pab par mgyur bar bye padang bu med pa la sa pa'i grus
18a1(dkon brtsegs): mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya bar myi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing dpag tu mchis
18a2(dkon brtsegs): grangs ma mchis/ bsam gyis mi khyab / mtshungs pa ma mchis/ tshad ma mchis pa dang / sems can dag gis bdag gi ming thos par gyur la ming thos pa tsam gyis byang chub
18a3(dkon brtsegs): kyi snying po'i mtha'i bar du/ tshangs par spyod par gyur pa de srid dubadag bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par myi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das
18a4(dkon brtsegs): gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe phyogs bcu kun tu sangs rgyas kyi zhing dpag tu ma mchis grangs ma mchis bsam gyis myi khyab mtshungs pa ma
18a5(dkon brtsegs): mchis tshad ma mchis pa dag na sems can gang dgagis bdag gi myeng thos la yan lag lnga'i phyagabagyi bas phyag 'tshal ba dang / de dag byang chub
18a6(dkon brtsegs): sems dpa'a'i spyad pa spyod pa na lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis sti stang du bgyi bar ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs
18a7(dkon brtsegs): bar 'tshang brgya bar mi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na/ byang chub sems dpa' gang chos gos 'khru 'am/ skems sam
18a8(dkon brtsegs): 'drub pa'am/ 'tshed pa'i las bgyid par gyur la chos gos rin po che sar rapa khye'u tsang rigs bzang ba/ de bzhin gshegs pas gnang ba dag sems bskyed ma thag tu bgos par
18b1(dkon brtsegs): bdag gis 'tshal bar ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par myi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag byang chub thob pa'i tshe
18b2(dkon brtsegs): sangs rgyas kyi zhing der sems can dag skyes ma thag tu 'di lta ste/ dper na dge slong dgra bcom pa yongs su gdung ba ma mchis pa bsam gtan gsum pa la snyoms par zhugs pa lta bur
18b3(dkon brtsegs): bde ba rnam pa de lta bu thob par ma gyur pa de srid du/ bdag bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang brgya par myi bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das gal te bdag

24b6(dkon brtsegs): mog por byed pa'i 'od dang / mdor bsdus na 'od thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyind pa zhes bya'o// de 'od de ni dri ma myed pa shi nang tu brgyas pa/ lus la bde ba
24b7(dkon brtsegs): skyed pa// sems dga' bar byed pa/ lha dang / lha ma yin dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / nam mkha' lding dang / lto'i 'phye chen po dang / myi 'am ci dang / mye dang
24b8(dkon brtsegs): myi ma yin pa rnams la dga' ba dang / mchog tu dga' ba dang / bde ba skyed pa sems can dge ba'i bsam pa can rnams la dge ba dang / yang dag togs pa dang / mkhas pa dang
25a1(dkon brtsegs): blo dang mchog tu dga' ba byed pa'o// kun dga' bo rnam grangs 'dis sangs rgyas kyi zhing gzhan mtha' yas mu med pa dang de bzhin gshegs pas yongs su gang ste bskal
25a2(dkon brtsegs): pa de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag myed de'i mtshan gyi las rgyur byas pa dang / 'od phun sum tshogs pa las brtsams te/ brjod kyang mtshan bstand pa dang / 'od phun sum tshogs pa'i yon tan gyi mtha' yang rtogs
25a3(dkon brtsegs): par myi nus la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi 'jigs pa yang rgyu nad chad par myi 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kun dga' bo 'di lta ste// bcom ldan 'das 'od dpag myed de'i 'od kyi yon tan 'byor pa dang / de
25a4(dkon brtsegs): bzhin gshegs pa'i shes rab dang / spobs pa bla na med pa dang / de gnyi ga yang grangs myed/ dpag tu myed cing / bsam gyis mi khyab la mu med pa'i phyir ro// kun dga' bo de bzhin
25a5(dkon brtsegs): gshegs pa 'od dpag myed de nyan thos kyi dge 'dun dang / ga tu myed de/ nyan thos bye ba phrag 'di snyed cig ce'am nyon thos bye ba brgya phrag 'di snyed cig ci 'am/ nyan thos bye ba stong phrag 'di
25a6(dkon brtsegs): snyed cig ce 'am/ nyan thos bye ba brgya stong phrag 'di snyed cig ca'am/ gtams phrag 'di snyed cig ce 'am/ dkrigs phrag 'di skad cig ce 'am/ khrag khrig phrag 'di snyed cig ce 'am/ ther 'bum phrag 'di
25a7(dkon brtsegs): snyed cig ce'am/ mi 'khrugs pa phrag 'di snyed cig ce 'am/ rnam mdog phrag 'di snyed cig ce 'am/ rgyun 'bab phrag 'di snyed cig ce'am/ rgyal ba phrag 'di snyed cig ce'am/ dpag tu myed pa phrag 'di snyed
25a8(dkon brtsegs): cig ce'am/ grangs myed pa phrag 'di snyed cig ce 'am/ bgrang du myed pa phrag snyed cig ce 'am/ mtshungs pa myed pa phrag 'di snyed cig ce 'am/ bsam gyis myi khyab pa phrag 'di snyed cig ces de'i tshed gzung bar sra
25b1(dkon brtsegs): ba ma yin no// kun dga' bo 'di lta ste dper na/ dge slong me'u 'gal gi bu chen po rdzu 'phrul dang dbang thob pa// de 'dod na stong gsum gi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gi khams na/ skar ma'i gzugs ci snyed yod pa de dag
25b2(dkon brtsegs): thams cad nyin thos zhag gcig gis bgrang ba de lta bu'i rnam pa'i rdzu 'phrul dang ldan pa/ bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong yod par gyur la/ de dag las gzhan mi byed par lo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du de bzhin gshegs
25b3(dkon brtsegs): pa 'od dpag med kyi nyan thos dang po 'dus pa bgrangs kyang / de dag gis brgya'i char yang bgrangs par myi 'gyur te// stong dang / brgya stong dang / cha dang dpe dang / rgyu'i bar du yang bgrangs par myi 'gyur ro// kun dga'
25b4(dkon brtsegs): bo 'di lta ste dper na/ rgya mtsho chen po zabs su dpag tshad brgyad khri bzhi stong yod pa khyon dpag tu myed pa la myi la la zhig gis sgra tshal ba brgyar bshags pa'i rtse mos chu thigs pa cig blangs na/ kun dga' bo de 'di
25b5(dkon brtsegs): snyam du sems/ gang skra tshal pa brgyar bshags pa'i rtse mos chu thigs pa gcig blangs pa dang / gang rgya mtsho chen po'i chu'i phung po phyi na las pa de gnyis gang mang / gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das
25b6(dkon brtsegs): dpag tu stong yang rgya mtsho chen po bas nyung lags na/ skra tshal pa brgyar bshags pa'i rtse mos chab thigs pa gcig blangs pa lta ci smos kyang ci tshal/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa
25b7(dkon brtsegs): kun dga'o chu thigs pa gcig lta bu ni/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag myed kyi nyan thos dang por 'dus pa la me'u 'gal gi bu'i dge slong rnams kyis lo bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du bgrangs
25b8(dkon brtsegs): te/ 'di snyed gcig go zhes grangs kyis chod pa lta bu ma yin no// rgya mtsho chen po'i chu'i phung po phyin las pa lta bu ni grangs kyis mchod par blta ba yin na// nyan thos 'dus pa gnyis pa dang gsum pa rnams lta
26a1(dkon brtsegs): smos kyang ci dgos te/ bcom ldan 'das de'i nyan thos kyi dge 'dun ni de ltar mtha' yas mu med de/ de ni dpag tu myed do zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro ba yin no// kun dga' bo bcom ldan 'das de
26a2(dkon brtsegs): bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag myed de'i tshe'i tshad kyang dpag tu med de/ bskal pa 'di snyed cig ce'am/ bskal pa brgya phrag 'di snyed cig ce 'am/ bskal pa stong phrag 'di snyed cig ce'am/ bskal pa brgya stong
26a3(dkon brtsegs): phrag 'di snyed cig ce'am/ bskal pa bye ba phrag 'di snyed cig ce'am/ bskal pa bye ba brgya phrag 'di snyed cig ce'am/ bskal pa bye ba stong phrag 'di snyed cig ce'am/ bskal pa bye ba brgya stong phrag
26a4(dkon brtsegs): 'di snyed cig ce'am bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig 'di snyed cig go zhes bya ba'i bar du de'i tshad rtogs par sla ba ma yin no// kun dga' bo bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag med de'i sku
26a5(dkon brtsegs): tshe'i tshad de ltar dpag tu myed pa de/ de'i phyir de bzhi na gshegs pa de tshe dpag myed ces bya'o// kun dga' bo ba com ldan 'das de de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag myed de/ bla na myed
26a6(dkon brtsegs): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzog sa par sangs rgyas nas/ ji ltar da ltar 'jig te nang gi kha mas 'di na bskal pa grangs dang / bskal pa bgrang ba'i brdar btag
26a7(dkon brtsegs): pa de lta bu'i bskal pa bcu lon no// kun dga' bo bcom ldan 'das 'od dpag myed kyi 'jig te nang gi khams bde ba can zhes bya ba'i/ 'byor pa med pa/ bde ba/ lo legs pa/ nyams dga'
26a8(dkon brtsegs): ba/ lha dang mye mang po gang ba'o// kun dga' bo 'jig te nang gi khams de na/ sems can dmyal ba myed do// dud 'gro'i skye gnas myed do// yi dgas kyi yul myed do// lha ma yin gyi ris
26b1(dkon brtsegs): myed do/ myi khom pa myed do/ 'jig te nang gi khams bde ba can na snang ba'i rin po che gang yin pa de dag ni 'jig rte nad na myi spyod do// kun dga' bo 'jig rte nang gi khams bde ba can de ni spos sna tshogs dri
26b2(dkon brtsegs): rab tu zhim pa'i ngad ldang ba'o// me tog dang 'bras bu sna tshogs 'byor pa'o// rin po che'i shing ljon pas legs par brgyan pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pas sprul pa'i bya sna tshogs sgra yid du 'ong
26b3(dkon brtsegs): can gyi tshogs kyi bstend pa'o// kun dga' bo rin po che'i shing ljon pa de dag ni kha dog tha dad pa/ kha dog tu ma pa/ kha dog dum brgya stong phrag du ma yod pa'o// kun dga' bo don rin po che'i shing ljon pa
26b4(dkon brtsegs): gser gi kha dog lta bu dang // gser ga rang bzhin dag yod do dngul gi kha dog lta bu dang / dngul gi rang bzhin dag yod do// be dur+ya'i kha dog lta bu dang / be dUr+ya'i rang bzhin dag yod do// shel gi kha dog lta bu dang
26b5(dkon brtsegs): shel gyi rang bzhin dag yod do// spug gi kha dog lta bu dang / spug gi rang bzhin dag yod do// mu tig dmar po'i kha dog lta bu dang / mu tig dmar po'i rang bzhin dag yod do// rdo'i snying pol
26b6(dkon brtsegs): kha dog lta bu dang / rdo'i snying po'i rang bzhin dag yod do/ kha cig ni gser dang / dngul dang / rin po che sna gnyis pa dag yod do// gser dang / dngul dang / be dur+ya dang / rin po che sna gsum pa
26b7(dkon brtsegs): dag kyang yod do// gser dang / dngul dang / be dur+ya dang / shel dang / rin po che sna bzhi pa dag kyang yod do// gser dang / dngul dang / be dur+ya dang / shel dang / spug dang / rin po che sna lnga pa dag kyang yod do// 
26b8(dkon brtsegs): gser dang / dngul dang / be dur+ya dang / shel dang / spug dang / mu tog dmar po dang / rin po che sna drug pa dag kyang yod do// gser dang / dngul dang / bye du rgya dang / shel dang / spug dang / mu tig dmar
27a1(dkon brtsegs): po dang / rdo'i snying po dang rin po che sna bdun pa dag kyang yod do// kun dga' bo de na gser gi shing ljon pa rnams kyi ca rje/ sdong po dang 'i yal ga dang / lo ma dang / 'das
27a2(dkon brtsegs): mA dang / me tog rnams gser gi rang bzhin la/ rtsa ba rnams dngul gyi rang bzhin no// dngul gri shing ljond pa rnams kyi rtsa ba dang / sdong po dang / yalu gi dang / lo ma dang / 'dab ma dang /

27a5(dkon brtsegs): rnams shol gyi ring bzhin la/ 'bras bu rnams spug gi rang bzhin no// spug gi shing ldan pa rnams kyi/ rtsa ba dang / sdong po dang / yal ga dang / lo ma dang / 'dab ma dang / me tog

27a8(dkon brtsegs): ga dang / lo ma dang / 'dab ma dang / me tog rnams rdo'i snying po'i rang bzhin la/ 'bras bu rnams gser gi rang bzhin la no// kun dga' bo shing ljon pa kha cig ni rtse ba rnams
27b1(dkon brtsegs): gser gi rang bzhin la/ sdong po rnams dngul gyi rang bzhin/ yal ga rnams bye dur+ya'i rang bzhin/ lo rnams shel gyi rang bzhin/ 'dab ma rnams spug gi rang bzhin/ me tog rnams mu tig
27b2(dkon brtsegs): dmar po'i rang bzhin 'bras bu rnams rdo'i snying po'i rang bzhin no// kun dga' bo shing kha cig ni rtsa ba rnams dngul gyi rang bzhin la/ sdong po rnams bye dUr+ya'i rang bzhin/ yal ga rnams
27b3(dkon brtsegs): shel gi rang bzhin/ lo ma rnams spug gi rang bzhin/ 'dab ma rnams mu tig dmar po'i rang bzhin/ me tog rnams rdo'i snying po'i rang bzhin// 'bras bu rnams gser gi rang bzhin
27b4(dkon brtsegs): no// kun dga' bo shing ljon pa khri cag ni rtsa ba rnams bye du r+ya'i rang bzhin la/ sdong po rnams la shel gyi rang bzhin yal ga rnams spug gi rang bzhin/ lo ma
27b5(dkon brtsegs): rnams mu tog dmar po'i rang po zhen/ mdab ma rnams ngo'i snang po'i rang bzhin/ me tog rnams gser gi rang bzhin/ 'dra sa bu rnams dngul gyi rang bzhin no// kun
27b6(dkon brtsegs): dga' bo shing ljon pa kha cig ni rtsa ba rnams shel gyi rang bzhin la/ sdong po rnams spug gi rang bzhin/ yal ga rnams mu tig dmar po'i rang bzhin/ lo ma rnams rdo'i snying po'i rang
27b7(dkon brtsegs): bzhin/ mdab ma rnams gser gi rang bzhin me tog rnams dngul gi rang bzhin/ 'bras bu rnams bye dUr+ya'i rang bzhin no// kun dga' bo shing ljond pa kha cig ni rtsa ba rnams spug

28a1(dkon brtsegs): me tog rnams bye dUr+ya'i rang bzhin 'bras bu rnams shel gyi rang bzhin no// kun dga' bo shing ljond pa kha cig ni rtsa ba rnams mu tig dmar po'i ring bzhin la

28a3(dkon brtsegs): rang bzhin 'bras bu rnams spug gi rang bzhin no// kun dga' bo shing ljon pa kha cig ni rtsa ba rnams rdo'i snying po'i rang bzhin la/ sdong po rnams gser gi rang bzhin
28a4(dkon brtsegs): yal ga rnams dngul gyi rang bzhin/ lo ma rnams bye dUr+ya'i rang bzhin// mdab ma rnams shel gyi rang bzhin me tog rnams spug gi rang bzhin 'bras bu rnams mu tig dmar
28a5(dkon brtsegs): po'i rang bzhin no// kun dga' bo shing ljond pa kha cig ni rtsa ba rnams rin po che sna bdun gi rang bzhin la sngon po rnams kyang rin po che sna bdun gi rang bzhin/ yal
28a6(dkon brtsegs): ga rnams kyang rin po che sna bdun gi rang bzhin lo ma rnams kyang rin po che sna bdun gi rang bzhin ma dab ma rnams kyang rin po che sna bdun gi rang bzhin me
28a7(dkon brtsegs): tog rnams kyang rin po che sna bdun gi rang bzhin 'bras bu rnams kyang rin po che sna bdun gi rang bzhin no// kun dga' bo shing ljond pa de dag thams cad kyi rtsa dang / sdong
28a8(dkon brtsegs): po dang / yal ga dang lo ma dang 'dab ma dang me tog dang / 'bras bu rnams ni/ 'jam pa reg na bde ba dri zhim pa dag go// rlung gyis bskyed
28b1(dkon brtsegs): de dag las bstand cing yid du 'ong ba'i sgra 'byung ste/ bstand pa dang / mthun zhing mnyan pas chog mi shes pa'o// kun dga' bo sangs rgyas kyi zhing de ni rin po che sna bdun gyi shing
28b2(dkon brtsegs): ljond pa rnam par de lta bu dag gis gang ste/ mtha' na rin po che sna bdun gyi chu shing gi sdong po dang / rin po che'i shing ta la'i 'phreng ba gis yongs su bskor to// thams cad kyang
28b3(dkon brtsegs): gser gi dra bas khebs pa'o// kun tu rin po che sna bdun gi pad ma rnams kyis khebs pa'o// de na pad ma'i tshad dpag tshad phyed pa tsam yang yod do// dpag tshad kyi tshad tsam yang
28b4(dkon brtsegs): yod/ dpag tshad gcig dang / gnyis pa dang bzhi pa/ dang / lnga'i tshad tsam yang yod/ dpag tshad bcu'i b.ragyi tshad tsam dag kyang yod do// rin po che'i pad ma thams
28b5(dkon brtsegs): cad las kyang 'od gzer bye ba stong phrag sum bcu rtsa drug drug 'byung ngo // 'od gzer gyi rtse mo thams cad las kyang sangs rgyas sku gser gi kha dog can/ skyes bu chen po

28b7(dkon brtsegs): sems can rnams la chos stond te/ de bzhin du lho dang / nub dang / byang gi phyogs dang / 'og dang steng dang / phyogs mtshams rnams su 'jig rte nad gi khams tha dad pa/ grangs myed
28b8(dkon brtsegs): dpag tu myed pa dag tu gshegs nas/ sems can rnams la chos ston to// kun dga' bo sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na rin po rnams ye myed do/ ri thams cad kyang rin po che'i ri sha stag go// rig
29a1(dkon brtsegs): rgyal po ri rab thams cad dang / 'khor yug dang / ri'i rgyal po khor yug chen po thams cad dang / rgya mtsho chen po rnams byed do/ nisangs rgyas kyi zhing da ni kun tu mnyam pa
29a2(dkon brtsegs): nyams dga' ba/ lag 'thil ltar mnyam pa/ sa phyogs rin po che rnam pa sna tshogs kyis spros pa'o// de skad ces bka' stsal po dang / bcom ldan 'das la tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos 'di skad ces
29a3(dkon brtsegs): gsol to// bcom ldan 'das rgyal chen bzhi'i ris kyi lha'i ri rab kyi ngos la gnas pa dang / sum bcu rtsa gsum pa'i ri rab kyi rtse mo la gnas pa de dag gang na gnas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
29a4(dkon brtsegs): stsal pa/ kun dga' bo 'di ji snyam du sems/ 'di ni ri'i rgyal po ri rab kyi gong ma mtha' bral gi lha rnams dang / dga' ldan dang / 'phrul dga' dang / gzhan 'phrul dbang byed dang
29a5(dkon brtsegs): tshangs ris dang / tshangs pa mdun na 'don dang / tshangs chen las 'og myin gyi bar gyi lha rnams gang na gnas/ gsol pa bcom ldan 'das las kyi rnam par smin pa dang // las mngon
29a6(dkon brtsegs): par 'du bgyid pa bsam gyis myi khyab pa// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal da pa/ kun dga' bo las kyi rnam par smind pa dang / las mngon par 'du byed pa bsam gyis myi khyab pa ni rnyed par rung gyi/ 
29a7(dkon brtsegs): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba dang / rdzu 'phrul dang / byin gis rlabs bsam gyis myi khyab pa ni sus kyang mtha' 'am tshad rtogs pa 'am/ bsam pararo myi nus te/ gzhan du na
29a8(dkon brtsegs): sangs rgyas kyi yul bsam gyis myi khyab po zhes rab tu 'byed do// de ltar sems can bsod nams byas pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa/ bsod nams dang // ye shes dang / rdzu 'phrul dang / 'byor
29b1(dkon brtsegs): pa bsam gyis myi khyab pa dang sangs rgyas kyi zhing der 'byung ngo // gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das bdag ni de la dogs pa 'am/ yid gnyis sam/ the tsom ma mchis te/ bdag ni ma 'ongs pa'i sems
29b2(dkon brtsegs): can rnams kyi dogs pa dang / yid gnyis dang / the tsom bstsal ba'i slad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa la don 'di yongs su zhu'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsald pa/ kun dga' bo legs so legs so// 
29b3(dkon brtsegs): ngalta bu ni khyod kyi bya ba yin no// kun dga' bo 'jig te nang gi khams bde ba can de na/ chu klung rnam pa sna tshogs dag 'bab ste/ den chu klung chen po kha tshon dpag tshad tsam dag yod/ dpag tshad bcu'i dang / 
29b4(dkon brtsegs): shu dang / sum bcu dang / bzhi bcu dang / lnga bcu'i bar dang kha tshon dpag tshad brgya stong gi tshad tsam dag kyang yod de/ zab sa su dpag tshad bcu gnyis pa dag go// chu klung de dag thams cad kyang / 
29b5(dkon brtsegs): spos dri rab tu zhim pa sna tshogs kyi chur 'bab cing rin po che'i me tog sil ma'i tshogs dang / 'bab pa dag go/ sgra dbyangs snyand pa tha dad pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa dag go// kun dga' bo
29b6(dkon brtsegs): chu klung chen po de dag las lha'i klu dbyangs yan lag bye ba brgya stong dang ldan pa'i sil snyan dag mkhas pa rnams kyis byas pa bas lhag pa'i sgra yid du 'ong ba 'byung ste/ chu klung chen po de dag las rnam
29b7(dkon brtsegs): pa 'di lta bu'i sgra 'byung ba ni zab pa dang / kun shes par bya ba dang / rnam par shes par bya ba dang / brdzun ma yin pa dang / rna bar bde ba dang / snying du 'ong ba dang / dga' bar bya ba dang / snyan pa dang / yid du 'ong ba
29b8(dkon brtsegs): dang / mnyan pos chog myi shes pa dang / mnyand pa dang mthun pa dang / myi rtag pa dang zhi ba dang / bdag myed ces bya ba dang / mnyand na bde ba ste/ de dag sems can de dag gi rna ba'i dbang po la grag go/ 
30a1(dkon brtsegs): kun dga' bo chu'i klung chen po de dag gi 'gram gnyis ni rin po che'i spos kyi shing ljon pa dag gis gang ste// de dag la yal ga dang / lo ma dang / mye log/ kha dog sna 'tshogs 'phyang ngo // de nas sems can gang dag chu

36a3(dkon brtsegs): rgyumyur du zhing 'di rnam par blta bar 'gyur// rgya chen zhing 'dir lhags par gyur nas kyang // lha'i myig dang lha'i rna ba dang // tshe rabs dran dang blo gros mkhas mchog dang // rdzu 'phrul stobs kyang myur du thob par 'gyur// sangs rgyas

36a5(dkon brtsegs): mang dag na sems can 'ong // de dag nga'i zhing du lhags nas ni// de dag/ skye ba gcig las phyir myi ldog/ de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' gang zhig 'dir// bdag gi zhing yang 'di 'drar 'gyur ba dang / 
36a6(dkon brtsegs): bdag gyis mying dang sgra dang lta bas kyang // sems can mang po 'grol bar bya 'dod pa// de ni myur du rings par la gor du// bde ba can gi 'jig rtend khams song la// 'od dpag myed kyi gan du song nas ni// sangs rgyas
36a7(dkon brtsegs): bye ba stong la khyab mchod kyis// rdzu 'phrul stobs kyis zhing mang song nas ni// sangs rgyas bye ba mang la mchod byas te// bde bar gshegs la mchod pa byas nas kyang // dro khang bde ba can du slar yang 'ong // kun dga' bo de bzhin/
